A little house sits upon a hill. A mother, father and child sits around the dinner table ready to eat dinner. A knock on the door startles the family. The mother gets up from her chair and opens the door. At the steps lies you, a baby quietly sleeping in a cradle with a note reading, Last Hope. The mother is confused and takes you in to nurture you. The father and the child sit there stunned looking at you as to why you are in their home. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Why is that baby here? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Mama, why is that baby in our home? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' I don't know why they left him here. All was left was this note but I dont understand what it means. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' You didn't check around? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' No I did not see anyone else. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Alright, for now, we take care of the baby and treat him as our own. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' But we don't know his elemental power. How are we going to help him? What do we say when he grows up? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' That time will come when it does. For now we will take care for him. [[Looking for Help]]''You'' Hey, Dad. I am walking to the forest to explore. I'll be back soon! ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Before you go, you should walk with your brother alongside you. I don't want you getting lost or hurt. You prefer to walk alone but you wonder if you should have your brother walk with you to explore the forest nearby. Do you walk alone or walk with your brother? [[Walk Alone]] [[Walk with your Brother]] You are intrigued about this new elemental power you possess. It's unlike anything you ever seen or felt. You wonder how to access this power and how to wield it. You are unsure how to go about channeling this power. ''You'' Do i stick my hands out? Do i have to pose or something to use this power? Let me try sticking my hands out. You become curious to using your power as you try accessing your power. You rememeber seeing a fire elemental user stick out his hands to shoot out flames and balls of fire. You wonder if you could do the same. You start to stick your hands out. [[Stick hands out]] You feel a surge of power overflowing within your body. Its beyond anything you ever seen, your arms start pulsing with purple streaks and your hands glow with purple light. At it's climax, the purple light shoots out of your hands at fast speed towards a tree. You choose to walk alone into the forest gazing at the small animals running around and the nice plants and trees around you. You feel a sense of calm spiritually and feel one with the forest. You continue going down the forest until you start having a strange feeling. You look at yourself and you start to see hints of purple mist radiating very slightly in your body. You become curious as this could be a sign of your elemental power. You stand back away from your brother as he sticks his hand upwards palm facing up and a ball of water appears in his hand. Your brother shoots the ball of water into the air until it disappears. You are amazed at his power and ask him to do more. He puts his hands together and pull apart to create a string of water between his hands. He moves it around and around to then close his hands together removing the water completely. ''You'' So cool. I wish i could get my elemental power. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Time will come when it's your turn to get your power. We just have to continue waiting and see what the future holds. You both continue to walk down the forest until you start feeling weird. You can't explain it but you have the feeling. You wonder why you feel this way. He arrives in the main area of the town. He can hear people talking amongst each other. He looks to his left and sees people are buying products for their home. He looks to the right and see young children practicing their elemental power strength. There is a fire wielder and earth wielder sparring against each other. The Earth Child uses both of his arms to create mini walls to shoot back against the fire balls. This would continue as Father continues to watch this. The father is interested in watching the battle to see how the young fire wielder performs against the earth wielder. He knows that fire and earth cancel each other out at the advanced level of mastery. However, at young ages he knows each side can overpower the other with high knowledge to outwit your opponent. Father demonstrates by sticking his arm out to create a fire ball. The ball shoots from his hand towards an open area and uses his fingers to flick them to the right. The ball responds to this going right instead of straight. Then Father flicks upwards and the fire ball shoots up in the air to dissipate in the atmosphere. The two are in awe as they are amazed by Father's control over his fire elemental power. ''(text-colour:red)[Fire Child]'' Whoa, so cool! How did you do that? ''(text-colour:green)[Earth Child]'' Yea, how did you do that sir? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' It's all within your finger and control. You must learn to gain control over your elemental power to perform tricks with your power. This becomes useful when you are up against your opponent. ''(text-colour:red)[Fire Child]'' Thank you sir! I will keep this in mind and try to do that in the future. Come on, lets go. ''(text-colour:green)[Earth Child]'' Thank you sir for the tip. Goodbye now! The pair run off somewhere else in the town as Father waves goodbye to the pair and continues to walk into the town to find the seer. [[Find Seer]]Father keeps walking down the path of the town and eventually finds the seer's building. He enters the building and finds the seer reading up on papers and books to learn new tricks that elemental powers can perform. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Hello, are you free right now? ''Seer'' Well, yes I am free right now. What can I be of service to you? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I have this little baby who was left at my doorstep of my home. No one was around and it seems whoever had him just abandoned him for us to take care of. We are unsure of his elemental power and was hoping if you can come back to my home to check his power. ''Seer'' Ah I see. Well let's see what I can do. There are different ways for me to tell someone's power by distinct features that the baby has to determine it's elemental power. Shall we leave? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes please. The sooner we figure this out, the sooner we can hopefully find those who can care for the child and who shares his elemental power to teach him. [[Leave with Seer back to Home]]Father chooses not to help the Fire Child and continue walking down the town to find the seer. He believes that sometimes the children has to figure it out on their own or else babying someone won't improve their skill level and strength to master their elemental power. [[Find Seer]] The two men starts walking back to Father's home where Mother and their Child is home for the day. After some time walking, they eventually reach the home and walk inside to find Mother relaxing on the couch. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Love? I am home. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Why hello my love. I see you brought the seer home. Can you help us sir? ''Seer'' Yes, I can help you two with the child. Now where is the young fellow? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Yes, he is over here in this cradle that we found him in. ''Seer'' I see, now let me check him out. The seer picks you up and begins to check your features to find signs of distinct elemental features that are specific to an elemental power to distinguish what power a user has. ''Seer'' Hmm, I can't find any clues yet. The seer possesses the Earth elemental power but retrained himself using books to grant himself extensive knowledge of the elemental powers. He wanted to assist others in determining what their elemental powers are. When a child is born between 2 different elemental parents, it is often difficult for the parents to figure out what power their child possess. The power doesn't usually begin to show until the child reaches young adolscence of the ages of 8-12 where they can properly handle using their power. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Are you able to find any clues yet? ''(text-colour:green)[Seer]'' I am unsure. This is very unusual that the child doesn't have any distinct features that will tell me the boy's elemental power. I would advise going to the Elemental Tree back in Fourgrove. There aren't any markings that could be used to identify any elemental power. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' So what does that mean? Does the boy not possess any elemental powers at all? ''(text-colour:green)[Seer]'' Well it is possible. There are some cases of this happening to others so I wouldn't be too suprised if this was the case for the child. However, in those cases, some people were able to gain their elemental powers later than usual so I would take him to the Elemental Tree to get a answer from there. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Thank you Seer for your help, we appreciate it. ''(text-colour:green)[Seer]'' No problem. I am sorry that I could not find an answer. I did the best I could. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' It's alright Seer. We will go to the Elemental Tree now to get our answer, thank you for your help. The Seer waves goodbye and leaves the home to return to the town. Mother and Father discuss their options. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Well shall we go to the Elemental Tree? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I don't think we have a choice otherwise. Their Child runs down the stairs to ask what happened downstairs. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Mom, who were you guys talking to? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Hey honey, we were talking to a local seer who was trying to help us with the baby we found yesterday. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' What power does the baby have? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' We don't know son. We are going to the Elemental Tree to find out. Would you like to come with us? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Yes, I wanna come with you guys. Can I? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Why yes you can sweetie. We can see how your skill level is now. The family starts to get ready and brings you along to the Elemental Tree in Fourgrove. Fourgrove is the local town that the family lives near and was named under the Elemental Tree nearby that represents the unity of the 4 elemental powers living in harmony. The 4 elemental powers that the Tree united is Fire, Water, Earth and Air. [[Leave to Elemental Tree]]Mother holds you for the walk to the Elemental Tree as Father is holding the Child's hand on the way. After some time has passed, they eventually reach the Elemental Tree. The Tree vibrates with different colors and gives off a low hum. Markings show on the bark of the tree spiraling up to the top. The leaves alternate with different colors representing the 4 elements living together representing unity. The Child is filled with excitement trying to go near the tree to determine his skill level. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' I wanna go up to the Tree and see my skill level. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Okay honey, go up to the Tree and wait for its response. The Child walks up to the Tree and stands in front. The Tree gives off a soft hum and shakes slightly. Energy flow comes up from the base of the Tree like a shining light within the tree radiating off. The light goes up to the top and in an instant, the tree gives off streaks of blue colors representing the elemental power, Water. The blue color begins to diminish until it falls below the half way mark of the Tree telling the Child that he is close to Intermediate Skill level but still technically in Novice Level. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Hooray! I am almost halfway on the Tree. I am getting stronger with my elemental power! ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Congrats honey! I am so proud of you. Mother brings you to the Tree and places you in front of the tree and steps back to avoid disrupting the reading of your elemental power reading. The Tree gives off a soft hum and slightly shakes as usual as it tries to read your elemental power. The Tree's energy flow begins to go up to the top of the tree and radiates brightly on the bark. However, the Tree isn't showing any color afterwards, its just staying bright white. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' What is going on? Why is the Tree not showing a color yet? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Mom, what is going on? I am scared. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Don't worry honey, I am sure there is a reason for this. The Tree is building up its energy till eventually the light cannot hold itself any longer and shoots the energy high in the sky giving off a loud hum for everyone in Fourgrove to hear and the light disappears within seconds and becomes silent. The Tree makes no sound and is not responding to you at all. The family is left speechless as to what has happened. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' What just happened? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I don't know. This has never happened before. Let me pick him up. Father runs to you to pick you up and take you away from the Tree. The Elemental Tree stands still and no hum is heard. The area is silent and the family notices something on the tree. A small area of the Tree is losing its texture and color. It turns out the Tree is losing its power and now has a small area of wilt on itself. The family are startled by this discovery and begins to leave the Tree back home. [[Return to Home]]The family starts to return home as people nearby are looking in the direction of the Elemental Tree where they came from. They start walking towards the Tree to figure out what happened. Other people ask the family if they know what happened. ''Person 1'' Hey, do you know what happened over there? I saw you guys come from the direction of the Elemental Tree. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' No, we have no idea as to what happened over there. We were startled by the noise and heading home. ''Person 2'' Alright, well we are going to check out what happened. ''Person 1'' Yea, I want to know what happened. Let's go. The 2 people leaves the family in the direction of the Elemental Tree and the family wastes no time going back to their home. Father and the Seer both go into Fourgrove to the Elemental Tree to tell the people what happened to it. In doing so, your identity is exposed and people will be wondering what you caused the Tree to react this way. Mother returns home with you and the Child. She sends the Child upstairs to his room and Mother looks outside her window questioning what has happened. She wonders what elemental power you will possess when you come of age but for now, that remains a mystery. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Well, are we going to talk about what happened today? ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Yes, we will. Hey Son, could you go upstairs to your room for me? Mother and Father has to talk about important things. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Child]'' Yes Mother, I will go upstairs now. The Child leaves to go upstairs and the parents begin to talk as you are in the room with them. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' What do we do with the baby? He just damaged the Elemental Tree and it was told that the Elemental Tree can't be damaged. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Yes I know of the tales and this is a big shock to me as well. I mean we don't even know his elemental power. It can't be one of the 4 elemental powers right? I mean, no user has ever caused the Elemental Tree to react like that. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Perhaps his power is an combination of 2 different elemental powers or more. It is unprecedented after all so we should consider any possibilities. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Yes I agree. I think it could that he possesses all of the elemental powers. I think the Tree would be able to read 2 elemental powers but again, I don't know if that is true because it hasn't happened yet. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' At this point, I don't know what it could be. It could be anything but as of now, let's make sure his identity is hidden. We can't let people know who he is and question his elemental power as we don't know what it is yet. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' I agree, let's do that. Mother and Father agree to keep your identity safe and will continue to raise you as if you were a child to them. Years pass by and you have grown older. You are informed about the elemental powers and how you don't possess a power yet. You are interested in what your power can be and you head out of your home to explore the forest nearby to be at peace. [[Fast forward to Age 15]] You awake inside your home on your couch as the doctor is healing your wounds you sustained from the blast you shot out. Father, Mother and Brother is all next to you relieved that you have woke up from your unconsciousness. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Thank god you are okay. I was worried that your condition would worsen and you wouldn't wake up. ''You'' Yea, sorry Mother. I guess I didn't know what I was doing. I'm sorry. (if:(history:)contains"Walk with your Brother")[''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' You think? I told you not to do that and yet you got yourself hurt. You are lucky that I was able to minimize the damage initially. ''You'' Sorry Brother, I guess I got ahead of myself since it was my first time wielding this power. I was too excited to try out my power and I hurt myself because of it. ] (else:)[''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Well you are lucky that we found you. I heard a loud boom and rushed out with Father to find you unconscious. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes, the damage you suffered was alot so if we didn't find you, then I think you could've died. ] ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Well luckily, I was called immediately to tend to your injuries and get you fixed up right quick. ''You'' Thank you doctor, I am thankful for your support. [[Head to Elemental Tree]]''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Well now since you possess your elemental power now, we must head to the Elemental Tree to see if it will respond now to your newfound power. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' But he just got fixed up. He shouldn't be moving around as much and he needs to rest. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Yes, I would recommend that he needs to get some rest or else he won't recover to his full state. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I understand but we need to figure out what the Elemental Tree will say when he stands before it. If we wait any time longer then he could injure himself again without any control over it and be a danger to others. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Let the boy rest. I'm sure he can rest for a few days before he goes to the Elemental Tree right? ''You'' It's okay Mother, I am fine and I feel capable of walking to the Elemental Tree now. I promise I will be okay to go there. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Are you sure? I would prefer if you rested before going. ''You'' Yes I am sure. Besides I am curious of what my elemental power is going to be now since I can use it. I want to know more about it the sooner I can. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' The rest of you, stay here until we come back. After we determine his power, I want to see it in action. [[FInd out Elemental Power]]The two of you leave to the Elemental Tree to figure out what is the name of your Elemental Power as well as the strength level you are currently at with your power. It is clear that your raw power is greater than anything else that others have wielded. The sheer strength to cause great destruction with little effort to most is terrifiying and it is essential to control this power or else you are a risk to everyone else in Fourgrove. You continue walking down into Fourgrove towards the Elemental Tree but you can't help but wonder if the Tree will give you the same response it did when you were a baby. (if:(history:)contains"Go into Fourgrove")[[Judge Eyes]] [[Continue to Elemental Tree]]As you go closer to the Elemental Tree, you see the people of Fourgrove doing their daily tasks in the town and they wave to you to welcome your presence. You wave again giving your greetings back and continue walking towards the Elemental Tree. Father looks relieved as he believed he made the right decision not revealing your identity back then when he wanted to tell the truth. ''You'' Is something wrong? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Nothing son, let's keep moving forward. [[Elemental Tree Conclusion]]Once you reached the Elemental Tree, you can't help but notice half of the Elemental Tree has wilted away and the process is starting to spread to the other side of the Tree. This process is extremely slow as the Elemental Tree is very powerful and durable to damage. It will take a while for the Elemental Tree to wilt away fully. However you waste no time to step in front of the Elemental Tree to await its judgment upon you. You hope you get a different response this time. ''You'' Do I just stand here and wait? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes, now let the Elemental Tree do it's thing. The Tree starts building energy within slowly to the top to which the area around you starts to shake. Sediments on the ground come up from the ground and is floating in the air. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' This is different now, something must be happening. The energy within the Tree is moving rapidly to which it then reaches to the top and shoots out into the sky. A long line of white energy goes into the sky and disappears. Then the ground stops shaking, the sediments fall to the ground and the two of you stand there confused as to why nothing happened. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Dammit, why did nothing happen this time again? I don't remember the dirt from the ground floating in the air last time. I was sure this time it would be different. [[Confusion]]As you go closer to the Elemental Tree, you can't help but notice other people whispering amongst themselves as you pass by. They don't seem to recognize you at first but it is clear that your presence isn't welcomed in Fourgrove. You can't help but wonder why they don't appreciate you being here. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Ignore them son. I may have told them about what happened when you stood before the Elemental Tree. ''You'' Why? What happened? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' The Elemental Tree acted differently and weirdly, it was unlike anything I've ever seen before. After everything, I notice the Elemental Tree started to wilt and we were afraid of what was happening so we ran away back home. However, a friend convinced me to go with them to explain the situation of what was happening and sadly, the people of Fourgrove didn't take it well. I was hoping they would. ''You'' But if I didn't possess a Elemental Power before, then why did the Elemental Tree react weirdly if there was nothing to analyze? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Beats me but come on, we have to keep going and ignore the people around. The two of you keep moving forward trying to ignore everyone judging you as you pass by towards the Elemental Tree. [[Elemental Tree Conclusion]]Then, the wilting process starts to speed up rapidly, as the dark color begins to cover more of the other side of the Elemental Tree. It continues like this for a few minutes and stops. The wilting process is 60% complete and it seems that there isn't a solution to fix the wilting process or else it would be fixed already. ''You'' Father, is that supposed to happen? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes, after you stood before the Elemental Tree when you were a baby, others went in front of the Tree and it increased the speed of how fast the wilting process continues on the Elemental Tree. We agreed that we would reduce how often we step in front of the Tree but it seems that you make this process even faster. It's not your fault but when others go in front, the wilting process speeds up for a few seconds and slows down again. I don't know why but this is the situation we are dealing with right now. ''You'' Oh I see, I'm sorry for doing damage to the Tree then. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Save your sorrys' son, it isn't your fault that this is happening. We couldn't have known why the wilting process started. Suddenly a purple mist begins to float around the Elemental Tree. ''You'' What is happening Father? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Be quiet, let's see what happens. It surrounds the area that you stand in then all of the purple mist begins to float towards the Elemental Tree surrounding it entirely. You can see energy build up within the Tree itself repeating the process again. It reaches to the top and disappears. Energy falls to the bottom of the Tree revealing its answer to you. You also see the purple mist start to inscribe something onto the Tree for you to see then it disappears after. [[Aether]]''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' What did it say? I didn't get a chance to look. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Aether? I assume that's my elemental power name. It's a cool name for a powerful elemental power to have I guess. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Look at the energy within. It seems that you are at Novice level which is expected but your strength... The strength level shown on the Elemental Tree is way beyond Master level. For a user to wield such raw power and doesn't require any extensive training to push their strength level that high is absurd. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Wow, I didn't know it was that high. I thought Master level was the highest that people could achieve? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' That is what everyone assumed. I have never seen someone's strength level to be higher than Master level. This is very unexpected. [[Report Back Home]](set: $strengthCounter to 0){(if: (passage:)'s tags contains "strength")[(set:$strengthCounter to $strengthCounter + 1)]}The two of you rush back home to report what the Elemental Tree has told you. Once you have arrived, you see Mother, Brother, and the doctor talking to each other on the couch and turn to you as soon as you arrive. ''(text-colour:navy)[Mother]'' Hey guys! What did the Elemental Tree say? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Turns out his Elemental power is called Aether. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Aether? That is a interesting name to have. Did you guys name it? ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' No, this purple mist appeared and surrounded the Tree and spelt that word out for us. We assumed that word was the name for my elemental power. But this made the wilting process speed up quicker than others so the Tree has taken more damage now. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Its to be expected. The wilting process increases when someone steps in front to determine their power, strength and mastery. How long did this process last though? ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' A few minutes. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' A FEW MINUTES? Every other time is a few seconds. This Aether power must be the real deal then. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' That is truly shocking. A few minutes of rapid wilting is unnerving. That is bad since this means the Tree has sustained great damage now. It sucks since we don't have an answer to reverse this process. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' So what can we do for the Tree? ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' As of now, nothing. We don't know how to reverse the process so its best that you refrain from stepping in front of the Elemental Tree moving forward. We must try to use the Elemental Tree as much as we can before its inevitable death. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Well we have no time to waste now. We must train you to practice Aether. The sooner you learn to control your power, the sooner that you won't be a threat in everyday life. Doc, will you be willing to help us by being on standby during this training? We need someone to help us if anyone was to get hurt. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' It would be my pleasure. I will offer this service to be free as it would be in my best interests to ensure he doesn't hurt anyone else by accident because he can't control his power. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Then it's settled. I'll go into Fourgrove to hopefully find other Elemental users assist us in the training. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Who will you find Father? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I don't know yet but hopefully anyone willing to help. I will help you as well as your brother but the doctor should not help us. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Why not? ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Because my Elemental power is limited to heal others. I have taken on the form to heal others through Earth. However, my strength level has been reduced significantly to accept this form. I cannot go into combat as I would be an easy target to get rid of. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I see, it would be powerful if Earth could have high offense and healing capabilites in combat. Amongst the 4 elements, Earth would be the best right? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Just because your power is greater than others doesn't make you better. Earth would technically be better if that was the case but the other 3 elements can think of strategies to counter Earth users. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Yes, and well my healing powers take some time to perform so even if I had high offense capabilities, I would be hindered if I tried to heal in battle. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Okay, enough talking for now. I'm going into Fourgrove to find others. The rest of you stay here. I will be back soon. [[Recruit Anybody]]Father goes out into Fourgrove to hopefully find anybody that is willing enough to help you in your training. He goes to person to person and they are unwilling to help him as they have their own things to tend to. It seems that he will be unsuccessful in finding more people to help him in your training but he spots 2 users in the distance. He recognizes that the 2 users happen to be the 2 young children that he saw battling when he was trying to find the Seer. (if:(history:)contains"Fire Child Assistance")[[Acceptance]] [[Denial]]Father walks up to the 2 elemental users and asks for their help. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Hello you two. I am unsure if you remember me but I was the one who helped you I believe in teaching a trick with your Fire Elemental Power. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' Hmmm. Oh wait, yes I remember. I appreciate that tip alot. I was able to win battles against this one because of it. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Hello sir, how have you been? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I have been well. I have a question to ask you both. Are you two willing to help my son train his elemental power? His case is a special one as he just learned to wield his power and we need all the help he can get to train it. His strength is beyond anything I have ever seen and he is a threat to others if he can't control it. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' He just learned it recently? Interesting, what elemental power is it? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Well that's the thing. It isn't any of the 4 elemental powers. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' It isn't? Then what is it called? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Aether. It's a purple elemental power that shows tremendous raw power to the user who wields it. The problem is that he wasn't able to control this when he was younger like everyone else. It technically is a good thing because this power would be even worse given to a child. We need to help him control this power soon or he could hurt himself or others. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' I see. Well I am willing to help you in his training. You helped me back then when you had no need to, it's the least I can do to return the favor. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Yes I agree, we would like to repay your kindness forward by doing this for you. We are both in to help. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' That is great now I would like to find an Air user to help us. We have 3 out of the 4 elemental powers assisting and having Air would help us. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' I know an Air user nearby. Let me ask him. [[Find Air User]]Father walks up to the 2 elemental users and asks for their help. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Hello you two. I am hoping that you two are willing to help my son in training his elemental power? ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' Sorry sir, we don't know who you are and I find it strange that your son needs training. Wouldn't he be done with it by now? ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Yea, we already practiced our powers and we were able to reach Advanced level quickly in our adolescence so why hasn't your son done the same? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Well his power is a special case. It's unlike the 4 elemental powers. His is unbelievably stronger than Master level. It's called Aether. We need people to help him control it. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' You want us to help you? If this so called Aether power is stronger than Master level and he doesn't even know how to control it? That's suicide for us man. We could be killed in training if he can't control his power. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Sorry sir, but we value our lives and we don't want to lose it because we tried to help your son train his elemental power especially when he can't control it so we would be risking our lives for your benefit. We decline your offer. The two users leave and Father is discouraged that the pair left. He can't blame them as it makes sense that anything could happen when trying to help you in your training. [[Last Chance]]The Grown Earth User spots the Air user and asks him to help in your training of Aether. He summarizes what Father told them two and he offers his help as well. Father successfully was able to find others willing to help that will benefit your training greatly. The 4 of them start return back home and everyone introduces themselves quickly and Father gathers everyone and brings them out to an area isolated far from Fourgrove. This is to ensure that any damage caused won't affect anyone nearby to get accidentally injured. Mother wishes you goodbye and you repeat it back. [[Begin Group Training]]Father tries to find anyone who is willing to help you in your training. Then he stumbles across an Air user who is optimistic to help you in your training. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Hello sir, will you be willing to help my son in his training? He needs immediate help in training or else he can be a threat to himself and others. ''Air User'' Sure, I don't mind to help. Is your son young and you want him to learn from higher ups? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' No, he's 15 and he got his elemental power recently. ''Air User'' Recently? What power does he have? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Aether. It's this purple like elemental power that is powerful than all of the 4 elements combined. ''Air User'' Really? Well I would like to help. Anything to help a fellow person in our community. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I appreciate this a lot. The more help he gets, the better. The pair walks back to the house and the Air user introduces himself to the family. Father explains that he was unable to find any helpers but one. Luckily this user is an Air user so it will be beneficial to your training. Mother wishes everyone good luck in your training as she stays behind to do activities around the town. Father brings everyone to an isolated area far from Fourgrove to ensure any damage caused won't affect anyone. [[Begin Training]]''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Alright son, try channeling your elemental power. Close your eyes and control your breathing. Everyone else be on standby. You obey and try to channel your power. You feel nothing at first but then you feel energy starting to build within. You feel energy reaching your arms and you open your eyes to see purple mist surrounding your body and purple streaks run across your arms. You raise your hand again like before and a purple ball is formed at the palm of your hand. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' NOW HOLD IT. Father yells out loud to you. He is trying to make you control the purple ball and see how long you can control withholding your attack for. You try to hold it but you are struggling alot to do so. The physical strength you have is decreasing rapidly and you know you can't hold the ball for so long. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I can't hold it much longer! ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Don't worry, the Air user and Brother will help you. You guys ready? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Yes, I am ready. ''Air User'' Me too. Brother starts to form a water shield around your purple ball hoping to reduce as much damage as possible and minimize the force of impact. The Air User is on standby to redirect the purple ball upwards to reduce any destruction caused by the purple ball as much as possible. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Now release it once Brother forms the water shield around it. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I can't hold it anymore! I have to let go! ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Okay release it! You release the purple ball outwards as you lack the physical energy to keep holding it at the palm of your hand. Brother was almost able to cover the purple ball but is unable to as he didn't have enough time to do so. The Air user is caught off guard by the shear speed that the purple ball is going at but is able to shoot out high pressure wind to force the purple ball to go upwards. The purple ball shoots up in the air from the redirect and Brother is trying to maintain the shield around the purple ball. Then the purple ball explodes causing everyone to lose their balance on the ground as the shockwave from the ball was released. Little purple bits falls from the sky but disappears from the wind in the air. Everyone is shocked to see how strong the purple ball attack was. Something so small and easy to perform can do such destruction and give tremendous power on attacking. The doctor runs over to remove any exhaustion you have from trying to hold the purple ball. You feel reenergized from the doctor's assistance. [[Hesitation]] ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Alright son, try channeling your elemental power. Close your eyes and control your breathing. Everyone else be on standby. You obey and try to channel your power. You feel nothing at first but then you feel energy starting to build within. You feel energy reaching your arms and you open your eyes to see purple mist surrounding your body and purple streaks run across your arms. You raise your hand again like before and a purple ball is formed at the palm of your hand. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Now son, try to hold it for as long as possible. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Are you sure? It's taking a lot of energy to even hold this power. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes, I want to see how long you can hold that for before releasing it. This is good practice for you to learn as it will be critical to hold your attacks before sending them out randomly. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I'll try but this is draining me fast. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Don't worry brother, I am here to help. Brother starts to form a water sphere around the purple ball to reduce its power on impact. The Air user is in awe watching this new elemental powers' attacks. He has never seen anything like this. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Air user, you must be ready to redirect his attack. ''Air User'' Redirect? I don't even know if my power will work on his. What if I fail? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Don't doubt yourself, you can do it. Now son, release the ball. Be ready Air User. You release the purple ball and it shoots out quickly towards a little grassy hill. Brother maintains the water sphere around the purple ball to reduce its power and the Air user tries to redirect the purple ball upwards. He attempts and fails to redirect as the purple ball was too fast for him to redirect. The purple ball connects with the grassy hill and causes it to explode into pieces going everywhere. The shockwave causes the elemental users to lose their balance as the ground beneath them shakes violently for a moment then stops. Dirt pieces falls from the sky towards the ground from the explosion causing it to fly everywhere. [[Air User leaves]]It can't be helped that the Air User, Grown Earth User and Grown FIre User are worried for their lives now. They are shocked from the power you demonstrated and they are hesitant to continue your training as they could seriously get hurt from your attacks. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' Uhhh, I don't know if I want to continue helping. That attack was unbelievable. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Yea, that attack is daunting to me and I don't know if I want to continue. And that was with all the extra precautions taken to reduce its impact and destruction. ''Air User'' Yea, it was tough to even redirect the purple ball. What if I wasn't ready and the ball made contact with the ground or nearby trees? The destruction would be tremendous. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Listen you three, I understand your concern but we must help my son to train his power. If we don't do this then imagine him walking through Fourgrove possessing this power that he can't control. I'm sorry to say this but he is a threat to everyone else if he can't control Aether. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' I hear you sir but knowing this, I don't think I will reside in Fourgrove any longer after this. Just knowing the possibility that your son can cause mass destruction or even his presence in Fourgrove is a major threat to me. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Listen, I get it that you 3 are scared. Trust me I am scared too. To know that my brother wields Aether which is a extremely powerful elemental power that has no bounds of resistance is terrifying. But if we don't help him train, then lives will be at risk everytime when he walks into Fourgrove. Think about the potential lives that could be lost because we didn't do this now. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' Yea I understand. It's just that I never seen such raw power be so strong. I've seen a few cases of Master strength power be done and this is beyond anything that is even comparable to that. I can't live with my conscious knowing I let people die because I didn't help. I'm back in. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Yea I don't think I could live with myself with that outcome. ''Air User'' Same, I was scared thinking about my own life but there are others who would be at risk if we don't help. I'm not scared anymore. It is critical that you can use your power longer so you aren't tired from doing one attack. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I guess that makes sense. Okay then, who am I against? ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' First one to land an attack on the other wins the duel. Can you blame the guy? I would leave to if I was him as well. I only stay here because its clear that I must stand by to heal any injuries that you guys sustain. I can't stand by and let people get injured knowing I could've been there to stop the pain quickly. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' We appreciate it Doc, but now it'll only be the 3 of us training and it will progress slower to do so. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' I understand. I wish I could help but it will reduce my healing power considerably so if you guys take major damage, I'm afraid that I won't be able to heal your major injuries. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' It's okay Doc, I wish I wasn't in the position I was now of having this power but sadly it is what it is. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Correct. Life is unpredictable in many ways but we must accept the situation at hand and proceed onwards. [[Resume Training]]''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' I guess we will have to train your power by ourselves. Now I want you to spar with your Brother for the time being and then it will be the both of us. Now the two of you, get ready. You and Brother get together and turn around to go 20 steps back from each and turn around to face each other. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Ready, set...GO! Brother launches a quick water ball at you and you barely dodge out of the way. He then launches two more water balls at you and since you don't want to get hurt, you cross your arms making an X in front of you to take the damage on your arms instead of your body. The water balls connect but instead of damaging you, you absorb his attack and you feel empowered within. You decide to launch an attack back at him and he dodges it with ease. He sticks the landing but the impact of your attack causes Brother to lose his balance and you rush quickly to capitalize his mistake. You connect to his back sending him flying back to the ground. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' STOP! Son, are you okay? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Yes I am okay. I formed a shield where he was trying to strike and it reduced the damage I would've taken from his attack. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' HEY, next time you do a attack, make sure you dont try to kill him. He's your brother after all. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I'm sorry Brother. I will try to limit my power as best as I can. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Don't feel sorry, I understand. You can't control it and it's gonna take a while now let's go again. You launch a rapid fire attack against Brother to which he gets out of the way. You decide it is a good idea to shoot a mini purple ball near the ground where Brother is so he can lose his balance and you can do an sneak attack on him. [[Grown Fire User Battle]]The Fire User combines his hands together to form a laser type attack against you to which you counter by shooting a purple ball back at him. The laser disappears as the purple ball is powerful enough to render opponent's attacks useless. The Fire User dodges out of the way to avoid the attack and sticks the landing. However, the purple ball hit another grassy hill causing the earth nearby to shake making him lose his balance. You take this opportunity to strike and catch him off guard. You rush towards him with Aether in your hand but you are mentally trying to limit this power as much as you can before connecting to his body. Alright that concludes the one on one battles and it's time for the 5v1 battle now. We will give everything we got against you Son so don't hold back. You know yourself that you won't hold back whatsoever. You don't want to lose again. You want to win. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Okay Father! Everyone besides you and the Doctor are lined up next to each other getting ready to charge their elemental powers to use against your attack. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Whenever you are ready son, shoot out an powerful attack against us and we will counter but don't stop till I tell you too, you got that? ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I understand Father! You already plan on not losing this battle to begin with anyways. You are going to win this one whatever it takes. [[5v1 Battle]]You start by doing your purple ball attack. However, you focus on holding this attack longer but also trying to make it stronger. The purple ball starts to get bigger and bigger to which you cannot hold it much longer and release towards the group. The ball moves with pace towards them despite its size and the group unleashes their full power against the purple ball. At first, both sides are equal in power but the purple ball seems to be overpowering the group. Then they let out their battle cries as they empower themselves up to wield increased strength in their elemental powers and the purple ball is now being pushed back towards you. You refuse to accept this and you pour everything you got into the purple ball. You refuse to lose for the 5th time in a row and you are fueled with energy and determination to win this battle. You are pouring all of your strength into this attack and the purple ball is now being pushed towards the the group. You look like you are going to win this battle but their resistance is even stronger now. You are now losing this fight. You mutter to yourself... <img src= "https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQprUshlDahSnOwOKbwuUAFaxLtJeWvNUfFfA&s"> ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Impossible. How are they doing that? No, I'm not losing again, I can't! I won't! You feel more empowered as your feelings influence your power greatly and you use this to your advantage. The purple ball is now going towards the group. You hear Father trying to yell out... ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Okay Son...enough. You can... attack...stop.... You couldn't hear what he was trying to say but you ignore it as you are fueled with anger and some sense of hatred. You cannot let yourself down so you are putting everything you got into this attack. You cannot lose, you won't allow it. You keep going and putting more power in the attack then suddenly the earth beneath you is shaking. You can't keep up putting more power into the attack as you lose balance as the shaking intensifies more and you fall over. Then you hear Father yell... ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' NOW! The Purple ball is redirected upwards with great force from the group and goes high in the sky and with the high pressure winds from the Air User forces it higher to avoid any damage caused from the expected explosion. Then the Air User uses more wind to push you towards the group as the Grown Earth User forms a shield over the group and you see the Doctor also with the group as well. Then a loud BOOM is heard in the sky as its roar echoes on the landscape. You hear the noise of flames falling down and trees are catching fire. The Grown Earth User hold this shield for a few minutes and lets go causing it to disappear into bits and crumbles. The training grounds is littered with purple flames all over the grass and nearby trees. Brother and the Air User rush out to put the flames out and try to prevent as much damage as possible. You ask Father what has happened. [[Feelings]]''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' You weren't letting up on your attack. I suppose you couldn't hear me talk to you over the noise being generated by all of our attacks combined so I had the Doctor helped us out. ''(text-colour:green)[Doctor]'' Yes, I had to use some of my strength of my elemental power to shake the ground enough to make you fall to the ground and luckily, the stance you took when doing your attack was poor so I was able to get you off your footing and stop you from putting more additional power into the purple ball. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Yes, it was lucky he succeeded or else we could've been killed by your attack or at least taken major damage. You need to be careful when performing your attacks Son. I understand you don't want to lose the battle but you can't let your feelings consume you. Feelings play a major role in your elemental power's offensive capabilities. If you don't control them, you will be a major threat to deal with and all of this training would be for nothing if you don't control your feelings. ''(text-colour:red)[Grown Fire User]'' Agreed. Believe me as when I was letting my feelings get out of hand, I exerted tremendous fire power and burnt the surrounding grass and trees into crisps and dust. Luckily, I had my friend help me out and calm me down. ''(text-colour:green)[Grown Earth User]'' Yes, I was able to reduce his fire power and make sure that he was kept in check. The environment however was nothing but black tint over it. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I see. I'm sorry guys, I didn't mean to let my feelings get the better of me. I just hate to lose and after losing easily and quickly, I really wanted to win this battle and didn't notice the power I was giving in that purple ball. Brother and the Air User finish up putting out all of the fires and return back to meet up with the group. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Hey brother, maybe next time you get riled up, don't let it out on us? You could've hurt us. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' I'm sorry Brother. I just got too much into the moment, I won't do it again. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Agreed. I think that is enough training for today. We need to find another area to train as this land is destroyed. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Sorry Father. I didn't mean to do that. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' It's okay Son. We will continue your training until you get used to it. It will take time so don't feel the need to rush it. You will control your power eventually. The group leaves back to Fourgrove as the training for today is over and they will repeat this for the next few years. [[Fast forward to Age 19]]Its been a few years after you begun your training. You gotten the hang of using Aether and you are no longer a threat to the people of Fourgrove anymore. You are able to use your power at will and you learned to control it while not letting your feelings get the better of yourself. Its a normal day at the home and you are helping Mother around the house with chores. You hear Brother at the door call for your name. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Hey brother, come here now. You need to come with me at Fourgrove now. You stop what you are doing and follow Brother. The two of you rush towards Fourgrove but on the way there, you see a dark cloud in the sky above what seems to be over the ocean nearby. ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Father is waiting for us there. He told people in Fourgrove to evacuate immediately. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' Why? Is this an emergency? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' Unsure but he said he had a bad feeling about it. He consulted the local Seer about your power now since it was becoming mastered but the Seer mentioned to him that your power was going to be put to the test and the results can be devastating. He assumed this was the moment so everyone in Fourgrove is evacuated now. It's just us 3 for now. ''(text-colour:purple)[You]'' What happened to the people we know who helped with my training? ''(text-colour:cyan)[Brother]'' They are helping their relatives evacuate and it is unknown if they will come back to help handle the situation. [[Figure]]The score is 1-0 with you winning. You are happy that you succeeded in landing an attack on Brother and you are motivated to keep going. ''(text-colour:red)[Father]'' Alright, get ready...get set...GO! You form a purple ball attack to launch at Brother but you try to reduce this attack as much as possible so you don't hurt him. You try to control youself but the purple ball disappears from your attempt of trying to limit the damage. Brother then launches a water ball at you so you try to defend to empower yourself. The water ball hits your X and you feel empowered so you try to launch an attack and then another water ball strikes your chest as you let your guard down and you get pushed back down. Brother wins this battle against you.
